        <a class="question-hyperlink" href="/questions/160608/do-a-git-export-like-svn-export">
         Do a "git export" (like "svn export")?
        </a>
       </h1>
       <div class="ml12 aside-cta flex--item print:d-none sm:ml0 sm:mb12 sm:order-first sm:as-end">

         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I've been wondering whether there is a good "git export" solution that creates a copy of a tree without the
            <code>
             .git
            </code>
            repository directory. There are at least three methods I know of:
           </p>
           <ol>
            <li>
             <code>
              git clone
             </code>
             followed by removing the
             <code>
              .git
             </code>
             repository directory.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="http://www.kernel.org/pub/software/scm/git/docs/git-checkout-index.html" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git checkout-index
              </code>
             </a>
             alludes to this functionality but starts with "Just read the desired tree into the index..." which I'm not entirely sure how to do.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="http://code.google.com/p/git-export/" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git-export
              </code>
             </a>
             is a third-party script that essentially does a
             <code>
              git clone
             </code>
             into a temporary location followed by
             <code>
              rsync --exclude='.git'
             </code>
             into the final destination.
            </li>
           </ol>
           <p>
            None of these solutions really strike me as being satisfactory. The closest one to
            <code>
             svn export
            </code>
            might be option 1, because both require the target directory to be empty first. But option 2 seems even better, assuming I can figure out what it means to read a tree into the index.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">
           <div class="post-taglist d-flex gs4 gsy fd-column">

                <code>
                 git archive --format zip --output "output.zip" master -0
                </code>
                will give you an uncompressed archive (-0 is the flag for uncompressed).
                <a href="http://git-scm.com/docs/git-archive" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                 git-scm.com/docs/git-archive
                </a>

             <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
              <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
               <span class="comment-copy">
                I concur with @mrTom, and I don't think whether the archive is compressed or uncompressed is the main issue. With SVN, I can
                <code>
                 export
                </code>
                a 250 kB subdirectory directly from remote repository (which could otherwise be 200 MB in size, excluding revisions) - and I will only hit the network for 250 kB (or so) download transfer. With
                <code>
                 git
                </code>
                ,
                <code>
                 archive
                </code>
                has to be enabled on server (so I can't try it) -
                <code>
                 clone --depth 1
                </code>
                from server may still retrieve a repo of say 25 MB, where the
                <code>
                 .git
                </code>
                subfolder alone takes 15MB. Therefore, I'd still say answer is "no".
               </span>
               <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                –

        <a name="163769">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="163769" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2511" id="answer-163769" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="163769">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="2511" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             2511
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/163769/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Probably the simplest way to achieve this is with
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/git-archive" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git archive
              </code>
             </a>
             . If you really need just the expanded tree you can do something like this.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive master | tar -x -C /somewhere/else
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Most of the time that I need to 'export' something from git, I want a compressed archive in any case so I do something like this.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive master | bzip2 &gt;source-tree.tar.bz2
</code></pre>
            <p>
             ZIP archive:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --format zip --output /full/path/to/zipfile.zip master 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <a href="https://git-scm.com/docs/git-archive" rel="noreferrer">
              <code>
               git help archive
              </code>
             </a>
             for more details, it's quite flexible.
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             Be aware that even though the archive will not contain the .git directory, it will, however, contain other hidden git-specific files like .gitignore, .gitattributes, etc. If you don't want them in the archive, make sure you use the export-ignore attribute in a .gitattributes file and commit this before doing your archive.
             <a href="http://feeding.cloud.geek.nz/2010/02/excluding-files-from-git-archive.html" rel="noreferrer">
              Read more...
             </a>
            </p>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             Note: If you are interested in exporting the index, the command is
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout-index -a -f --prefix=/destination/path/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             (See
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/160719/413020" title="Greg's answer">
              Greg's answer
             </a>
             for more details)
            </p>
           </div>

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Be aware that the archive will not contain the .git directory, but will contain other hidden git-specific files like .gitignore, .gitattributes, etc.  So if you don't want them, make sure you use the export-ignore attribute in a .gitattributes file and commit this before doing your archive.  See
                 <a href="http://feeding.cloud.geek.nz/2010/02/excluding-files-from-git-archive.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  feeding.cloud.geek.nz/2010/02/…
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/17991/mj1531" title="1,966 reputation">
                  mj1531
                 </a>

                </span>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="4063443" data-comment-owner-id="102401" data-comment-score="57" id="comment-4063443">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="supernova" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 57
                </span>
               </div>

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 To follow up on Streams' note: you can add a '--prefix=something/' string into the command to control the directory name that will be packed inside the zip. For example, if you use
                 <code>
                  git archive --format zip --output /path/to/file.zip --prefix=newdir/ master
                 </code>
                 the output will be called 'file.zip' but when you unpack it, the top level directory will be 'newdir'. (If you omit the --prefix attribute, the top level dir would be 'file'.)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/102401/alan-w-smith" title="23,141 reputation">
                  Alan W. Smith
                 </a>
                </div>

                 The easiest way:
                 <code>
                  git archive -o latest.zip HEAD
                 </code>
                 It create a Zip archive that contains the contents of the latest commit on the current branch. Note that the output format is inferred by the extension of the output file.
                </span>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="160719">

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/160719/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I found out what option 2 means. From a repository, you can do:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git checkout-index -a -f --prefix=/destination/path/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The slash at the end of the path is important, otherwise it will result in the files being in /destination with a prefix of 'path'.
            </p>
            <p>
             Since in a normal situation the index contains the contents of the repository, there is nothing special to do to "read the desired tree into the index". It's already there.
            </p>
            <p>
             The
             <code>
              -a
             </code>
             flag is required to check out all files in the index (I'm not sure what it means to omit this flag in this situation, since it doesn't do what I want). The
             <code>
              -f
             </code>
             flag forces overwriting any existing files in the output, which this command doesn't normally do.
            </p>
            <p>
             This appears to be the sort of "git export" I was looking for.
            </p>
           </div>

                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/138023/znarkus" title="22,266 reputation">

                 </a>

                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">

                  Jun 24, 2010 at 16:55
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">

             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="6521402" data-comment-owner-id="26604" data-comment-score="35" id="comment-6521402">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="supernova" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 35
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 +1 to conny's advice.  Also, don't try to create '~/dest/', as this creates a directory called '~' in your working directory, rather than what you really wanted.  Guess what happens when you mindlessly type rm -rf ~
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/26604/kyle-heironimus" title="7,403 reputation">
                  Kyle Heironimus
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2011-04-18 16:38:22Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Apr 18, 2011 at 16:38
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="52571730" data-comment-owner-id="685715" data-comment-score="5" id="comment-52571730">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="warm" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 5
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @KyleHeironimus - your warning about using '~/dest/` is true iff you use quotes around your prefix path which tells the shell not to perform tilde expansion. A dir called
                 <code>
                  ~
                 </code>
                 (not
                 <code>
                  '~'
                 </code>
                 !) will be created in your working dir. There is nothing special about
                 <code>
                  git checkout-index
                 </code>
                 in this regard: The same is true of
                 <code>
                  mkdir '~/dest'
                 </code>
                 (
                 <i>
                  don't do that!
                 </i>
                 ). Yet another good reason to avoid file names that need quoting (e.g. that have a space in them) :-)
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/685715/matt-wallis" title="723 reputation">
                  Matt Wallis
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2015-09-02 09:18:23Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Sep 2, 2015 at 9:18
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 3 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">

                  </path>

              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <code>
              git archive
             </code>
             also works with remote repository.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --format=tar \
--remote=ssh://remote_server/remote_repository master | tar -xf -
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To export particular path inside the repo add as many paths as you wish as last argument to git, e.g.:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --format=tar \
--remote=ssh://remote_server/remote_repository master path1/ path2/ | tar -xv
</code></pre>
           </div>

                 <code>
                  git archive --format=tar --prefix=PROJECT_NAME/ --remote=USER@SERVER:PROJECT_NAME.git master | tar -xf -
                 </code>
                 (ensures your archive is in a folder)

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/19689284/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/p73W2.png"/>
            </p>
            <h3>
             A special case answer if the repository is hosted on GitHub.
            </h3>
            <p>
             Just use
             <code>
              svn export
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             As far as I know Github does not allow
             <code>
              archive --remote
             </code>
             . Although GitHub is
             <a href="https://github.com/blog/626-announcing-svn-support" rel="noreferrer">
              svn compatible
             </a>
             and they do have all git repos
             <code>
              svn
             </code>
             accessible so you could just use
             <code>
              svn export
             </code>
             like you normally would with a few adjustments to your GitHub url.
            </p>
            <p>
             For example to export an entire repository, notice how
             <code>
              trunk
             </code>
             in the URL replaces
             <code>
              master
             </code>
             (or whatever the
             <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/setting-the-default-branch/" rel="noreferrer">
              project's HEAD branch is set to
             </a>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn export https://github.com/username/repo-name/trunk/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And you can export a single file or even a certain path or folder:
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn export https://github.com/username/repo-name/trunk/src/lib/folder
</code></pre>
            <h3>
             Example with
             <a href="https://github.com/jquery/jquery" rel="noreferrer">
              jQuery JavaScript Library
             </a>
            </h3>
            <p>
             The
             <code>
              HEAD
             </code>
             branch or
             <strong>
              master
             </strong>
             branch will be available using
             <code>
              trunk
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn ls https://github.com/jquery/jquery/trunk
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The non-
             <code>
              HEAD
             </code>
             <strong>
              branches
             </strong>
             will be accessible under
             <code>
              /branches/
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn ls https://github.com/jquery/jquery/branches/2.1-stable
</code></pre>
            <p>
             All
             <strong>
              tags
             </strong>
             under
             <code>
              /tags/
             </code>
             in the same fashion:
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn ls https://github.com/jquery/jquery/tags/2.1.3
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 <code>
                  git://
                 </code>

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 You're right. I'd forgotten that I was using
                 <code>
                  git config url.&lt;base&gt;.insteadOf
                 </code>
                 to cache the remote repository. I was therefore using a
                 <code>
                  file://
                 </code>
                 URL in reality. I doubt that
                 <code>
                  git archive
                 </code>
                 could ever work with
                 <code>
                  git://
                 </code>
                 URLs since it needs to be able to run
                 <code>
                  git-upload-archive
                 </code>
                 at the remote end. It should be possible using the
                 <code>
                  ssh
                 </code>
                 protocol, except that github doesn't allow it (
                 <code>
                  Invalid command: 'git-upload-archive'
                 </code>
                 ).
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             From the
             <a href="http://www.kernel.org/pub/software/scm/git/docs/git-checkout-index.html" rel="noreferrer" title="Git Manual">
              Git Manual
             </a>
             :
            </p>
            <p>
             Using git-checkout-index to "export an entire tree"
            </p>
            <p>
             The prefix ability basically makes it trivial to use git-checkout-index as an "export as tree" function. Just read the desired tree into the index, and do:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              $ git checkout-index --prefix=git-export-dir/ -a
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="14296641" data-comment-owner-id="1079014" data-comment-score="4" id="comment-14296641">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 4
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 If you want to export directory foo in branch bar, then this would be
                 <code>
                  git read-tree bar:foo
                 </code>
                 And then
                 <code>
                  git checkout-index --prefix=export_dir/ -a
                 </code>
                 after that maybe you should do
                 <code>
                  git update-index master
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1079014/pascal-rosin" title="1,448 reputation">
                  Pascal Rosin
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2012-06-08 17:10:33Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">

                 </span>
                </span>

                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="209489" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="39" id="answer-209489" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="209489">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="39" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             39
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/209489/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I've written a simple wrapper around
             <code>
              git-checkout-index
             </code>
             that you can use like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git export ~/the/destination/dir
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If the destination directory already exists, you'll need to add
             <code>
              -f
             </code>
             or
             <code>
              --force
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Installation is simple; just drop the script somewhere in your
             <code>
              PATH
             </code>
             , and make sure it's executable.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="http://github.com/dasch/git-export/tree/master" rel="noreferrer">
              The github repository for
              <code>
               git-export
              </code>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="851113" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="36" id="answer-851113" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="851113">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="36" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             36
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/851113/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It appears that this is less of an issue with Git than SVN.  Git only puts a .git folder in the repository root, whereas SVN puts a .svn folder in every subdirectory.  So "svn export" avoids recursive command-line magic, whereas with Git recursion is not necessary.
            </p>
           </div>

                 </a>
                </div>

               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="35315638" data-comment-owner-id="143684" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-35315638">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="9416271" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="30" id="answer-9416271" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="9416271">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="30" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             30
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/9416271/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The equivalent of
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn export . otherpath
</code></pre>
            <p>
             inside an existing repo is
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive branchname | (cd otherpath; tar x)
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The equivalent of
            </p>
            <pre><code>svn export url otherpath
</code></pre>
            <p>
             is
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --remote=url branchname | (cd otherpath; tar x)
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="22702614">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="22702614" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="9" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="24" id="answer-22702614" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="22702614">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="24" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             24
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/22702614/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you're not excluding files with
             <code>
              .gitattributes
             </code>
             <code>
              export-ignore
             </code>
             then try
             <code>
              git checkout
             </code>
            </p>
            <pre><code>mkdir /path/to/checkout/
git --git-dir=/path/to/repo/.git --work-tree=/path/to/checkout/ checkout -f -q
</code></pre>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              -f
              <br/>
              When checking out paths from the index, do not fail upon unmerged
  entries; instead, unmerged entries are ignored.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             and
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              -q
              <br/>
              Avoid verbose
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Additionally you can get any Branch or Tag or from a specific Commit Revision like in SVN just adding the SHA1 (SHA1 in Git is the equivalent to the Revision Number in SVN)
            </p>
            <pre><code>mkdir /path/to/checkout/
git --git-dir=/path/to/repo/.git --work-tree=/path/to/checkout/ checkout 2ef2e1f2de5f3d4f5e87df7d8 -f -q -- ./
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The
             <code>
              /path/to/checkout/
             </code>
             must be empty, Git will not delete any file, but will overwrite files with the same name without any warning
            </p>
            <p>
             UPDATE:
To avoid the beheaded problem or to leave intact the working repository when using checkout for export with tags, branches or SHA1, you need to add
             <code>
              -- ./
             </code>
             at the end
            </p>
            <p>
             The double dash
             <code>
              --
             </code>
             tells git that everything after the dashes are paths or files, and also in this case tells
             <code>
              git checkout
             </code>
             to not change the
             <code>
              HEAD
             </code>
            </p>
            <p>
             Examples:
            </p>
            <p>
             This command will get just the libs directory and also the
             <code>
              readme.txt
             </code>
             file from that exactly commit
            </p>
            <pre><code>git --git-dir=/path/to/repo/.git --work-tree=/path/to/checkout/ checkout fef2e1f2de5f3d4f5e87df7d8 -f -q -- ./libs ./docs/readme.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This will create(overwrite)
             <code>
              my_file_2_behind_HEAD.txt
             </code>
             two commits behind the head
             <code>
              HEAD^2
             </code>
            </p>
            <pre><code>git --git-dir=/path/to/repo/.git --work-tree=/path/to/checkout/ checkout HEAD^2 -f -q -- ./my_file_2_behind_HEAD.txt
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To get the export of another branch
            </p>
            <pre><code>git --git-dir=/path/to/repo/.git --work-tree=/path/to/checkout/ checkout myotherbranch -f -q -- ./
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Notice that
             <code>
              ./
             </code>
             is relative to the root of the repository
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2014-03-28T01:39:03" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

                 </a>

            <p>
             I use git-submodules extensively.
This one works for me:
            </p>
            <pre><code>rsync -a ./FROM/ ./TO --exclude='.*'
</code></pre>

        <a name="8963061">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="8963061" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="11" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="20" id="answer-8963061" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="8963061">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="20" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             20
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/8963061/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I have hit this page frequently when looking for a way to export a git repository. My answer to this question considers three properties that svn export has by design compared to git, since svn follows a centralized repository approach:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              It minimizes the traffic to a remote repository location by not exporting all revisions
             </li>
             <li>
              It does not include meta information in the export directory
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Exporting a certain branch using svn is accomplished by specifying the appropriate path
              </p>
              <pre><code>git clone --depth 1 --branch master git://git.somewhere destination_path
rm -rf destination_path/.git
</code></pre>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             When building a certain release it is useful to clone a stable branch as for example
             <code>
              --branch stable
             </code>
             or
             <code>
              --branch release/0.9
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                 This does not work if the destination exists and is non-empty.

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="78172576" data-comment-owner-id="2809027" data-comment-score="2" id="comment-78172576">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 2
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 <b>
                  The One True Answer:
                 </b>
                 <i>
                  it arises from the depths.
                 </i>
                 The
                 <code>
                  git archive | tar
                 </code>
                 approach is inapplicable to POSIX-incompatible shell environments (e.g., AppVeyor's CMD- or PowerShell-based CI), which is non-ideal. The
                 <code>
                  git checkout
                 </code>
                 approach modifies the index of the main working tree, which is awful. The
                 <code>
                  git checkout-index
                 </code>
                 approach requires the index of the main working tree to be modified beforehand, which is even awful-er. The traditional
                 <code>
                  git clone
                 </code>
                 approach clones the entirety of the repository's history before deleting that history, which is wasteful. This is the only sane solution left.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/2809027/cecil-curry" title="8,905 reputation">
                  Cecil Curry
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2017-08-10 07:17:59Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Aug 10, 2017 at 7:17
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="78172851" data-comment-owner-id="2809027" data-comment-score="1" id="comment-78172851">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 1
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 To export locally, note that the absolute path of the Git working tree to be cloned from should be prefixed by the
                 <code>
                  file://
                 </code>
                 protocol (e.g.,
                 <code>
                  git clone --depth 1 --branch v3.14.15 file:///home/me/src_repo trg_repo
                 </code>
                 ). Failing to do so will emit
                 <code>
                  "warning: --depth is ignored in local clones; use file:// instead."
                 </code>
                 and perform a standard rather than shallow clone, defeating the entire purpose of this answer.
                 <i>
                  Salud!
                 </i>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/2809027/cecil-curry" title="8,905 reputation">
                  Cecil Curry
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">

                  Aug 10, 2017 at 7:24
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 3 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This will copy all contents, minus the .dot files. I use this to export git cloned projects into my web app's git repo without the .git stuff.
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              cp -R ./path-to-git-repo /path/to/destination/
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Plain old bash works just great :)
            </p>
           </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/19058735/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As simple as clone then delete the .git folder:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              git clone url_of_your_repo path_to_export &amp;&amp; rm -rf path_to_export/.git
             </code>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="25060822" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="14" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="12" id="answer-25060822" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="25060822">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/25060822/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For GitHub users, the
             <code>
              git archive --remote
             </code>
             method won't work directly, as
             <a href="https://developer.github.com/v3/repos/contents/#get-archive-link" rel="noreferrer">
              the export URL is ephemeral
             </a>
             .  You must ask GitHub for the URL, then download that URL.
             <code>
              curl
             </code>
             makes that easy:
            </p>
            <pre><code>curl -L https://api.github.com/repos/VENDOR/PROJECT/tarball | tar xzf -
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This will give you the exported code in a local directory.  Example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>$ curl -L https://api.github.com/repos/jpic/bashworks/tarball | tar xzf -
$ ls jpic-bashworks-34f4441/
break  conf  docs  hack  LICENSE  mlog  module  mpd  mtests  os  README.rst  remote  todo  vcs  vps  wepcrack
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Edit
             </strong>
             <br/>
             If you want the code put into a specific,
             <em>
              existing
             </em>
             directory (rather than the random one from github):
            </p>
            <pre><code>curl -L https://api.github.com/repos/VENDOR/PROJECT/tarball | \
tar xzC /path/you/want --strip 1
</code></pre>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="27788401">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

               </path>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27788401/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Yes,
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/163769/4221299">
              this
             </a>
             is a clean and neat command to archive your code without any git inclusion in the archive and is good to pass around without worrying about any git commit history.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --format zip --output /full/path/to/zipfile.zip master 
</code></pre>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I just want to point out that in the case that you are
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              exporting a sub folder of the repository (that's how I used to use SVN export feature)
             </li>
             <li>
              are OK with copying everything from that folder to the deployment destination
             </li>
             <li>
              and since you already have a copy of the entire repository in place.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Then you can just use
             <code>
              cp foo [destination]
             </code>
             instead of the mentioned
             <code>
              git-archive master foo | -x -C [destination]
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can archive a remote repo at any commit as zip file.
            </p>
            <pre><code>git archive --format=zip --output=archive.zip --remote=USERNAME@HOSTNAME:PROJECTNAME.git HASHOFGITCOMMIT
</code></pre>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="9475192" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="18" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="8" id="answer-9475192" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="9475192">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>

            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="8" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             8
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/9475192/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you want something that works with submodules this might be worth a go.
            </p>
            <p>
             Note:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              MASTER_DIR = a checkout with your submodules checked out also
             </li>
             <li>
              DEST_DIR = where this export will end up
             </li>
             <li>
              If you have rsync, I think you'd be able to do the same thing with even less ball ache.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Assumptions:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              You need to run this from the parent directory of MASTER_DIR ( i.e from MASTER_DIR cd .. )
             </li>
             <li>
              DEST_DIR is assumed to have been created. This is pretty easy to modify to include the creation of a DEST_DIR if you wanted to
             </li>
            </ul>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              cd MASTER_DIR &amp;&amp; tar -zcvf ../DEST_DIR/export.tar.gz --exclude='.git*'
  . &amp;&amp; cd ../DEST_DIR/ &amp;&amp; tar xvfz export.tar.gz &amp;&amp; rm export.tar.gz
             </p>
            </blockquote>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             My preference would actually be to have a
             <strong>
              dist
             </strong>
             target in your Makefile (or other build system) that exports a distributable archive of your code (.tar.bz2, .zip, .jar, or whatever is appropriate).  If you happen to be using GNU autotools or Perl's MakeMaker systems, I think this exists for you automatically.  If not, I highly recommend adding it.
            </p>
            <p>
             ETA (2012-09-06): Wow, harsh downvotes.  I still believe it is better to build your distributions with your build tools rather than your source code control tool.  I believe in building artifacts with build tools.  In my current job, our main product is built with an ant target.  We are in the midst of switching source code control systems, and the presence of this ant target means one less hassle in migration.
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="49238201">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="49238201" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="160608" data-position-on-page="20" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="8" id="answer-49238201" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="49238201">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="8" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             8
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/49238201/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             As I understand the question, it it more about downloading just certain state from the server, without history, and without data of other branches, rather than extracting a state from a local repository (as many anwsers here do).
            </p>
            <p>
             That can be done like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>git clone -b someBranch --depth 1 --single-branch git://somewhere.com/repo.git \
&amp;&amp; rm -rf repo/.git/
</code></pre>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               --single-branch
              </code>
              is available since Git 1.7.10 (April 2012).
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               --depth
              </code>
              is (was?)
              <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/23708231/git-shallow-clone-clone-depth-misses-remote-branches">
               reportedly
              </a>
              faulty, but for the case of an export, the mentioned issues should not matter.
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2018-03-12T14:53:19" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Bash-implementation of git-export.
            </p>
            <p>
             I have segmented the .empty file creation and removal processes on their own function, with the purpose of re-using them in the 'git-archive' implementation (will be posted later on).
            </p>
            <p>
             I have also added the '.gitattributes' file to the process in order to remove un-wanted files from the target export folder.
Included verbosity to the process while making the 'git-export' function more efficient.
            </p>
            <p>
             EMPTY_FILE=".empty";
            </p>
            <pre><code>function create_empty () {
## Processing path (target-dir):
    TRG_PATH="${1}";
## Component(s):
    EXCLUDE_DIR=".git";
echo -en "\nAdding '${EMPTY_FILE}' files to empty folder(s): ...";
    find ${TRG_PATH} -not -path "*/${EXCLUDE_DIR}/*" -type d -empty -exec touch {}/${EMPTY_FILE} \;
#echo "done.";
## Purging SRC/TRG_DIRs variable(s):
    unset TRG_PATH EMPTY_FILE EXCLUDE_DIR;
    return 0;
  }

declare -a GIT_EXCLUDE;
function load_exclude () {
    SRC_PATH="${1}";
    ITEMS=0; while read LINE; do
#      echo -e "Line [${ITEMS}]: '${LINE%%\ *}'";
      GIT_EXCLUDE[((ITEMS++))]=${LINE%%\ *};
    done &lt; ${SRC_PATH}/.gitattributes;
    GIT_EXCLUDE[${ITEMS}]="${EMPTY_FILE}";
## Purging variable(s):
    unset SRC_PATH ITEMS;
    return 0;
  }

function purge_empty () {
## Processing path (Source/Target-dir):
    SRC_PATH="${1}";
    TRG_PATH="${2}";
echo -e "\nPurging Git-Specific component(s): ... ";
    find ${SRC_PATH} -type f -name ${EMPTY_FILE} -exec /bin/rm '{}' \;
    for xRULE in ${GIT_EXCLUDE[@]}; do
echo -en "    '${TRG_PATH}/{${xRULE}}' files ... ";
      find ${TRG_PATH} -type f -name "${xRULE}" -exec /bin/rm -rf '{}' \;
echo "done.'";
    done;
echo -e "done.\n"
## Purging SRC/TRG_PATHs variable(s):
    unset SRC_PATH; unset TRG_PATH;
    return 0;
  }

function git-export () {
    TRG_DIR="${1}"; SRC_DIR="${2}";
    if [ -z "${SRC_DIR}" ]; then SRC_DIR="${PWD}"; fi
    load_exclude "${SRC_DIR}";
## Dynamically added '.empty' files to the Git-Structure:
    create_empty "${SRC_DIR}";
    GIT_COMMIT="Including '${EMPTY_FILE}' files into Git-Index container."; #echo -e "\n${GIT_COMMIT}";
    git add .; git commit --quiet --all --verbose --message "${GIT_COMMIT}";
    if [ "${?}" -eq 0 ]; then echo " done."; fi
    /bin/rm -rf ${TRG_DIR} &amp;&amp; mkdir -p "${TRG_DIR}";
echo -en "\nChecking-Out Index component(s): ... ";
    git checkout-index --prefix=${TRG_DIR}/ -q -f -a
## Reset: --mixed = reset HEAD and index:
    if [ "${?}" -eq 0 ]; then
echo "done."; echo -en "Resetting HEAD and Index: ... ";
        git reset --soft HEAD^;
        if [ "${?}" -eq 0 ]; then
echo "done.";
## Purging Git-specific components and '.empty' files from Target-Dir:
            purge_empty "${SRC_DIR}" "${TRG_DIR}"
          else echo "failed.";
        fi
## Archiving exported-content:
echo -en "Archiving Checked-Out component(s): ... ";
        if [ -f "${TRG_DIR}.tgz" ]; then /bin/rm ${TRG_DIR}.tgz; fi
        cd ${TRG_DIR} &amp;&amp; tar -czf ${TRG_DIR}.tgz ./; cd ${SRC_DIR}
echo "done.";
## Listing *.tgz file attributes:
## Warning: Un-TAR this file to a specific directory:
        ls -al ${TRG_DIR}.tgz
      else echo "failed.";
    fi
## Purgin all references to Un-Staged File(s):
   git reset HEAD;
## Purging SRC/TRG_DIRs variable(s):
    unset SRC_DIR; unset TRG_DIR;
    echo "";
    return 0;
  }
</code></pre>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              Output:
             </p>
             <p>
              $ git-export /tmp/rel-1.0.0
             </p>
             <p>
              Adding '.empty' files to empty folder(s): ... done.
             </p>
             <p>
              Checking-Out Index component(s): ... done.
             </p>
             <p>
              Resetting HEAD and Index: ... done.
             </p>
             <p>
              Purging Git-Specific component(s): ...
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.buildpath}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.project}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.gitignore}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.git}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.gitattributes}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{*.mno}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{*~}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.*~}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{*.swp}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{*.swo}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.DS_Store}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.settings}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              '/tmp/rel-1.0.0/{.empty}' files ... done.'
             </p>
             <p>
              done.
             </p>
             <p>
              Archiving Checked-Out component(s): ... done.
             </p>
             <p>
              -rw-r--r--  1 admin  wheel  25445901  3 Nov 12:57 /tmp/rel-1.0.0.tgz
             </p>
             <p>
              I have now incorporated the 'git archive' functionality into a single process that makes use of 'create_empty' function and other features.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <pre><code>function git-archive () {
    PREFIX="${1}"; ## sudo mkdir -p ${PREFIX}
    REPO_PATH="`echo "${2}"|awk -F: '{print $1}'`";
    RELEASE="`echo "${2}"|awk -F: '{print $2}'`";
    USER_PATH="${PWD}";
echo "$PREFIX $REPO_PATH $RELEASE $USER_PATH";
## Dynamically added '.empty' files to the Git-Structure:
    cd "${REPO_PATH}"; populate_empty .; echo -en "\n";
#    git archive --prefix=git-1.4.0/ -o git-1.4.0.tar.gz v1.4.0
# e.g.: git-archive /var/www/htdocs /repos/domain.name/website:rel-1.0.0 --explode
    OUTPUT_FILE="${USER_PATH}/${RELEASE}.tar.gz";
    git archive --verbose --prefix=${PREFIX}/ -o ${OUTPUT_FILE} ${RELEASE}
    cd "${USER_PATH}";
    if [[ "${3}" =~ [--explode] ]]; then
      if [ -d "./${RELEASE}" ]; then /bin/rm -rf "./${RELEASE}"; fi
      mkdir -p ./${RELEASE}; tar -xzf "${OUTPUT_FILE}" -C ./${RELEASE}
    fi
## Purging SRC/TRG_DIRs variable(s):
    unset PREFIX REPO_PATH RELEASE USER_PATH OUTPUT_FILE;
    return 0;
  }
</code></pre>
